Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Hwang Sun Jo
Reverend Sun Myung Moon, who at the age of 16 received a calling from Heaven for the salvation of humanity, has lived his entire life centered solely on the Heavenly Way. Reverend Moon described his life as follows:
"If Reverend Moon has any property, it is nothing but the suffering I endured for the public rather than for myself. In social life, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. In the providential position, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. …… Reverend Moon has been opposed and persecuted countless times by the nation and the world. I was opposed in America, by Christianity, Judaism, and even communism. Never in history has the world united to attack one person to eliminate him. In that sense, Reverend Moon is a global champion. 
However, despite being cursed, I did not crumble or perish. I emerged even stronger without the slightest tremor. …… Reverend Moon advocates for the liberation of humanity, the spirit world, hell, and even God." (Refer to Collected Speeches, Volume 105, pages 101-103)
In one word, Reverend Moon's life is 'suffering itself.' This suffering is not for himself but for God and humanity. Here, we come to know who he is. Reverend Moon is the Messiah and Savior that Christianity has hoped for over 2000 years, and he has come as the True Parent of humankind. Already, disciples following Reverend Moon in 185 countries worldwide are realizing the ideal of True Families with this confession of faith.
Reverend Moon's self-identity is verified through his words and life. He possesses a truth that does not exist in the world. The issues of God and humanity, history and the world, are clarified in his words. The promise of new words prophesied in the Bible is fulfilled in him, setting us free. These words contain 'life.' Moreover, more importantly, Reverend Moon's words are merely 'an interpretation of his own life.' In other words, he himself is the truth. The Word became flesh, that is, he incarnated. Therefore, life itself is the truth, and it approaches us through the framework of 'the Word.'
I am confident that readers will understand his greatness through Reverend Moon's words. The realm of Reverend Moon's words is so high and deep that it is immeasurable, but fundamentally, it has three characteristics.
First, through his words and life, Reverend Moon has revealed God. That is, he has liberated God from silence and suffering. Because humans have the bloodline of evil, they are children but cannot be called children, causing God's suffering. Reverend Moon has made the sorrowful God, who was tragically alienated due to human sin, 'speak.' He has made God, who was silent, trapped in church authority, doctrine, and splendidly decorated buildings, 'speak,' and he has made God, who could not come as the Parent of humanity, 'become the Parent,' thus Reverend Moon is 'God's complete revelation body.'
Secondly, Reverend Moon has liberated humans from ignorance and confusion. We humans have reasoning and can make value judgments, but we cannot deny the tragic reality that we have not fully explained our own existence. Moreover, humans are not independent beings but interdependent beings inseparable from others, yet we have not explained that relationship. The reason is that we have lost God's Word. Reverend Moon provides the ultimate answer to this. Furthermore, through a life that upholds the Heavenly Way, he shows a concrete model path. Therefore, his words are living words full of life.
Thirdly, Reverend Moon has liberated the world of all things. Every object created by God is an individual truth body with inherent value. Although its value should be fully realized under the dominion of the original human creation, it was not, and thus all things lamented. Reverend Moon has clarified the original value of the world of all things through his words and opened the way for the liberation of all things by restoring humans to their original state.
Reverend Moon and his wife, who have come as the eternal True Parents of humanity, continue to speak ceaselessly around the world today, demonstrating through their substantial lives the teachings of 'using the body of a servant with the heart of a parent' and 'living for the sake of others,' and striving to inherit true love, true life, and true lineage.
Furthermore, Reverend Moon, through the words of life, noble life, and achievements, has finally restored God's sovereignty as we enter the new millennium, settling as the King of Blessed Families on this earth. He has established the Peace UN, aiming for the Kingdom of Peace, Cheon Il Guk, the Fourth Israel, and is binding the world into one realm of heart.
I hope that the readers who encounter these words will become the owners of Cheon Il Guk and the main actors in building the Kingdom of Peace. *

You must not be ignorant of the reality of the spirit world 
『……Even if a small sin remains in oneself, one realizes that they cannot go before God, so they diligently seek out and cleanse their sins. And they are made to find a place they can go to again. When they visit the changed place, they strive even more to separate from evil spirits and shed their fallen nature to become absolutely good spirits. The path of indemnity is one you must go 
『Next is a lecture on ‘The Principle of Restoration.’ This lecture is conducted by Association President Yoo Ho-won. You will hear lectures on the providence of restoration centered on Adam's family, Noah's family, Abraham's family, Moses, and Jesus.』 
Blessed central families, having gone to the spirit world, know more than what they did on earth, so they try to teach even more. You don't even think about anything beyond knowing the principle on this earth, do you? You try to avoid and jump over it. You can't cross it. You must know that after crossing ten hills, a hundred more will rise higher. How will you solve that task? 
The path of indemnity is one you must go. 
If you are the owner of Cheon Il Guk, you must be a filial child in the house of Jehovah, centered on the kingdom of heaven, on behalf of God and the True Parents, and when you step outside, you must be a loyal subject in the nation, and the further you go into the distant world, the more you must increase your loyalty and filial piety. That is the cosmic world and the spirit world. You must know the range of activities that can expand infinitely to the center position and boundary line that can encompass the spirit world and claim sovereignty. Can you act without knowing? You must know this. You must memorize it clearly and know what position you are in, and you must know that it becomes a standard for criticism. Do you understand what I'm saying?「Yes.」 
Meeting the teacher and going doesn't mean you can be indifferent. You have things you must do. The many proclamations made by the teacher are not just passing clouds. Passing clouds gather to cause a flood. When a flood occurs, there is much damage. The spirit world is the same. Spirits who lived in the nation float around like clouds, and when they gather, there is damage like a flood. Wars also occur to settle everything. 
You can't be ignorant of indemnity. What have you indemnified by joining the Unification Church? If there is a difference between the life you lived before and the life you live now, you must know that the most important question is whether you have created a living environment with a substantial difference and are standing in the central position. 
Therefore, it's self-awareness, self-awareness! What is the fall? It's because they acted from a self-centered position, violating all of heaven and earth, that they fell into hell. Then, to fulfill the duties of a filial child, loyal subject, saint, and holy man in the Unification Church, you must have self-awareness, saying, ‘I will become such a person.’ To stand in the central position, you must have the ability to digest and freely create the environmental conditions. Only then can you feel self-awareness. Can being God's sons and daughters be achieved with words? You must have self-awareness as sons and daughters. 
Therefore, you must ask your conscience. Rather than thinking about the teacher, you must start from the unity of your body and mind. Even if you force yourself to go that path with differences, it won't work. It will be more difficult. If you come and go, enter and exit at will, it becomes more complicated. You must build a wall and climb up. You must place a ladder and climb up; the ladder won't pull you up. You must climb up yourself. The path of indemnity is unavoidable. Alright! 
To convert self-awareness into heavenly awareness, the principle is needed 
『Through the lecture, you will deeply understand how the central figures of the providence of restoration failed to fulfill their responsibilities, leading to the extension of the providence, and these situations are vividly displayed on the screen next to the podium, allowing the spirits to reflect on whether they committed such mistakes or wrongs in their past lives, leading them to cleanse their sins through reflection and repentance.』

God created with absolute love at the center. You must desire within love. Love desires to rise higher, and within that desire, there must be living for the sake of others. The saying that love is to invest and forget comes from this. It maintains the emotional standard. Absolute faith and absolute obedience maintain the path of true love at the horizontal position, rising higher and higher. 
Even in the world, to succeed, you must set a goal and invest on earth to achieve that goal, right? To succeed, you must study hard and invest on earth, just like there is an exam. To pass the standard of the exam process and achieve a great goal on earth, you must deny your environmental conditions and go. Only then does the denied environment provide self-awareness that establishes itself. 
The teacher is the same. How would the teacher feel the consciousness of being the Messiah and True Parents? When seeing the fact that the satanic world is defeated and retreats, and heaven and earth are harmonized, you must feel self-awareness, saying, ‘Ah, that's right!’ Self-awareness centered on heavenly principles! Satan had self-awareness centered on itself. How do you deny self-awareness and convert it into heavenly awareness? That's why the principle is needed. You must exchange it. You must have content to exchange it.

선생님이 가는 길 앞에서 진리의 문을 열기 위해서는 몇 시간이 아니에요. 24시간, 사흘 나흘을 철야하면서 뒤넘이쳤다는 사실을 알아야 돼요. 그런데 몇 시간도 못 참아? 그 따위 핑계도 하지 말라는 거예요. 그런 심각한 길을 개척한 통일교회가 가는 정도의 길은 어느 누가 침범하지 못해요. 내가 개척한 길은 영원히 남게 돼 있습니다. 하나님도 영원히 남으라고 보증, 보호하게 돼 있지, 그것을 갈려고 하게 안 돼 있다구요. 선생님 말씀은 영원히 가는 것입니다.

그들을 그냥 싸움하고 원수 취급할 것이 아니라, 기독교하고 모슬렘이 교차결혼해야 됩니다. 스털링스 주교인지 무엇인지 아들딸이 있으면 공산당의 아들딸하고 교차결혼하면 평화세계가 되는 거예요. 하늘이 이기게 돼 있어요. 선한 것이 이기게 돼 있기 때문에 하나의 세계가 되는 거예요.

교차결혼을 장려하는 것이 문 총재, 참부모의 소원입니다. 하나님의 소원입니다. 원해요, 안 원해요?「원합니다.」원하면 박수하라구요. (박수) 간단해요. 일본하고 한국의 수천 명을 내가 교차결혼시켰어요. 이놈의 간나 자식들, 자기들 멋대로 결혼하겠다고? 결혼도 하나님의 뜻 때문에 생겨난 거예요. 하나님이 기뻐할 수 있는 그 창조이상 가운데서 존재하는 것이지, 거기에서 벗어나 있을 수 없다는 사실을 알아야 돼요. 그렇기 때문에 하나님의 나라를 찾기 위해서는 무슨 짓을 못 해요? 무슨 짓을 못 해요? 나는 종의 종 입장에서 별의별 짓을 다했습니다.

자, 그만하면 이제 알 거예요. 그러면 이제 결론은 무엇이냐? 하나님의 나라가 없어요. 하나님이 나라를 가져 본 적이 있어요, 없어요? 통일교회를 중심삼고는 말이에요, 가정을 가져 봤고, 종족을 가져 봤어요. 완전하지 않지만, 아들딸이 훌륭하지 못하지만 불한당, 탕자라도 아들딸임에 틀림없어요. 그렇지만 가문이 어떻다는, 나라가 어떻다는 법이 나올 때는 그들을 다 시정해 가지고 바로잡을 수 있어요, 법만 나오게 되면.

나라가 없으면 선악을 가릴 수 없어 그렇기 때문에 통일교회 속에는 별의별 얄궂은 패들이 다 있지만 그건 문제가 아니에요. 법만 나오면 일시에 조정할 수 있기 때문에 다 품고 나간 것입니다. 문제는 뭐냐? 미국이 문제가 아니에요. 소련 공산당이 문제가 아니에요. 하나님이 원하는 나라가 있어야 됩니다. 하나님이 원하는 나라, 개인․가정․종족․민족․국가, 나라를 중심삼아 가지고 모델형이 있어야만 그걸 중심삼고 심판하는 거예요. 땅 위에 기준이 안 서게 되면 심판할 수 없어요. 비교해도 좋고 나쁜 것을 판단할 수 없습니다.

여러분, 공산주의자들은 말이에요, 김일성은 국가권 내에서 지옥 갔지만, 스탈린이라든가 레닌 같은 사람은 도망 다니고 있어요. 법이 없어요. 그건 세계적 주의 환경이니만큼 그 시대에 와 가지고 이제 선생님이 천일국을 중심삼은 법을 통해서 적용해야 재까닥 걸려 버린다는 거지요. 처리할 수 있는 방법이 다 나온다는 것입니다.

나라가 없으면 선악을 가릴 수 없습니다. 별의별 농간이 있어 가지고 힘이 부정적으로, 또 다음에 돈이 부정적으로, 그 다음에 권력이 부정적으로 하는 놀음을 중심삼고 팔고 사고 하는 놀음이 벌어지기 때문에, 사악한 세상으로 흘러가는 것이 더 빠르지, 선한 세상으로 돌아가는 것이 더 빠르지 않다는 사실을 아는 한 하나님의 나라를 복귀하는 것이 쉽지 않다는 사실을 알아야 돼요.

하나님이 나라를 만들지 못하게 돼 있어요. 그 나라를 잃어버리게 한 것은 참부모가 되지 못했기 때문입니다. 하나님이 자기 가정을 갖겠다고 못 하게 돼 있어요. 잃어버리게 한 것을 다시 참부모가 나와야만 가정으로부터 종족․민족․나라를 찾음으로 말미암아, 비로소 지옥의 나라를 청산해 버리고 천상에 비었던 나라를 한꺼번에 몇천년 빈 천국을 지금 몇 년 동안에 나라를 세워 가지고, 타락의 인연을 가진 개인․종족․민족․전세계 수천억이 지금 가서 머물고 있는 그 세계를 자리잡아 가지고 정비해서 다 맞춰 놓고 타락이 없었다 할 수 있는 결론을 지어 놓아야 하나님이 ‘다 이루었다!’ 할 수 있는 거예요.

이런 관점에서, 예수님이 겟세마네 동산에서 기도하면서 십자가에 돌아가게 될 때 ‘다 이루었다.’고 한 말이 무엇인지도 모르고, 꿈도 꾸지 못하고 그런 말을 하고 있다는 사실을 알아야 돼요.

문제는 뭐냐 하면 나라예요, 하나님이 원하는 나라. 이스라엘 민족을 통해 유대 나라를 중심삼아 가지고 로마를 수습할 수 있는, 모델적 국가 자체를 잃어버렸던 사실을 제2이스라엘권 미국을 중심삼고…. 미국이 제2이스라엘이라는 것을 모르고 있어요. 내가 가르쳐 주니까 알지요.

그러려면 완전히 같은 민족이요, 거기에서 흑인 백인이 싸울 수 없어요. 아시아인, 동양인, 무슨 구라파인, 그 다음에 아프리카인, 남미인 구별할 수 없어요. 평등 가치를 인정할 수 있는 국권이 못 돼 있으니 문제가 생기는 거예요. 그건 다 흘러가는 거예요.

이런 관점에서 보게 된다면, 이제 레버런 문이 지옥이나 모든 천상세계를 해방하여 평준화 시대에 들어왔기 때문에, 선생님이 가르쳐 준 말씀을 소련이 가져가면 미국의 복을 몽땅 빼앗아 가는 거예요. 옛날에 소련을 중심삼고 총칼로 만들었던 30개 가까운 국가를 한꺼번에 묶을 수 있어요.

그러한 엄청난 일이 통일교회 나라권 내에 있다는 사실을 알진대는, 얼마나 열심히 하고, 얼마나 귀하게 하루 생활과 자기 생애를 지내는 것이 아깝고 아까워 가지고 모든 것을 희생시키고 그 선두에 서지 않으면 안 되겠다는 자각을 갖고 살아야 할 텐데도 불구하고 방심을 하고 있어요! 제멋대로 놀음놀이하고 있다는 거예요.

요즘 뭐 크리스마스 시즌이 된다고 야단하고 그런데 말이에요, 크리스마스 데코레이션(decoration; 장식) 해서 뭘 해요? 예수가 좋아할 것 같아요? 통일교회 깃발을 꽂아 가지고 환영하는 것을 예수가 소원한다는 것을 누가 알아요? 모르는 사람들은 전부 지나가는 거예요.

기독교의 사상은 개인 구원이 아니라 나라 찾는 것 자, 그래서 나라가 필요하다는 것입니다. 하나님이 필요로 하는 그 나라가 있어야 되겠어요, 없어야 되겠어요? 어드래요?「있어야 됩니다.」그래, 여러분이 하나님이 원하는 나라의 백성이 되어야 되겠어요, 반대의 원수가 되어야 되겠어요? 백성이 돼야지요. 백성이 되겠어요, 그 나라의 황족이 되고, 그 나라의 왕자 왕녀가 돼야 되겠어요? 어떤 거예요?

하늘나라 왕궁의 왕자 왕녀로부터 황족이 결정돼 가지고 퍼져 나갈 수 있는 때를 놓쳐 가지고, 제멋대로 살다가 저나라에 가 보라는 거예요. 천대하고 우습게 여겼던 사람들이 저나라, 하늘나라의 왕자 왕녀, 황족이 돼 가지고 천상세계의 주인의 자리를 차지할 수 있는 것을 모르고 잃어버리는 불쌍한 무리가 선진국가들인 것을 알지어다! 경고합니다. 알겠어요?

미국 이 못난 사람들, 선진국이라고 자랑하지 말라구요. 프리 섹스가 뭐야? 호모가 뭐야? 드러그(drug; 마약)가 뭐야? 남자가 여자를 싫어하고, 여자가 남자를 싫어해 가지고, 향락에 떨어져 가지고 동물보다도 더 나쁜 무리가 하나님 앞에 설 수 있어요?

자, 그러니까 나라가 귀하니까 나라 귀한 것을 선포해야 돼요. 요전에 선생님이 유엔에 가 가지고 강연해 가지고 전세계 사람들이 전도, 전파해야 할 말씀의 내용을 남긴 거예요. 어느 누구도 관심을 안 갖기 때문에 내가 틀림없이 여기에서 가르쳐 줘야 되겠으니, 하나님이 찾는 나라가 어떻다는 것을 얘기하려는 이 아침인 것을 알고, 환영하고 기쁨으로 백 퍼센트 소화 흡수하겠다는 자신이 있는 사람들은 박수하고, 그렇지 않은 사람들은 일어서서 나가라구요. (박수)

박수들은 잘해요. 맹세문도 잘하지요. ‘맹세합시다!’ 얼마나 맹세를 많이 했는데, 한 번 실천해 봤어요?

기독교의 사상이 뭐냐 하면 나라를 찾는 거예요. 자기가 구원받는 것이 아니에요. 자기가 구원받아 가지고 자기 일족을 구원해 가지고 나라를 찾는 놀음이에요. 이것을 몰랐어요. 나라 찾는 그 칸셉이 있었더라도…. 미국 땅에 분파가 많아 가지고 수백 교회가 웬 말이에요? 있을 수 있어요?

나라 찾는 개념도 없는 기독교는 흘러가는 모래알같이 날아가 버린다는 사실을 알고, 이제는 알았으니 모래알이 진흙, 시멘트가 돼 가지고, 덩치가 돼 가지고 굴러가게 되면 천하가 다 깨져 나갈 수 있는 이런 힘을 갖추는 거예요. 나라를 건국해야겠다는 건국의 전통적 사실을 새로이 심어 놓지 않으면 미국도 날아가고 다 날아가요.

그런 의미에서 ‘나는 나라가 절대 필요하다.’ 하는 사람은 손 들어 봐요. 손들은 잘 드누만. 검은 손, 흰 손 다 손 드니까 다 비슷비슷하네. 자, 잘 들어요. 아시겠어요? 나라 찾는 일이 얼마나 귀한가를. 알겠어요?「예.」조는 사람이 있으면, 샤프 펜슬이 있지요, 샤프? 그걸 꽉 쥐고 눈을 감고 궁둥이를 찔러 대라구요. (웃음) 그래도 좋다고 하면 박수해 봐요. (박수) 박수 안 하는 사람은 일어서서 나가요. 그 옆에 그런 사람이 있으면 찔러대도 괜찮아요.

생각해 봐요. 목사라는 사람이 공석에 나서 가지고 이렇게 안 하면, 찔러서 안 되면 나가라고 누가 얘기하겠어요? ‘아이구, 어서 오소. 어서 오소!’ 하는 거지패들! 나 거지 패가 아니에요. 왕 패지요. 하나님이 왕을 시키겠다고 그랬지요, 아까? 그렇지요? 그런 거예요.

그 나라를 찾아야 하는 이유 자, 들어 봐요!『전국에서 모인 종교가…』다 종교가들이지요?『정치가, 학자, 지도자 여러분, 그리고 고명하신 평화대사 여러분!』여기에 평화대사들도 임명돼서 왔을 거라구요.

『오늘 여러분은 평화세계를 위한 소망을 품고 이 자리에 모였습니다. 본인은 이 뜻깊은 자리에서 세계평화초종교초국가초엔지오연합의 창시자로서 하나님이 본래 이상 하신 ‘하나님의 조국과 하나의 세계’에 관한 말씀을 전하고자 합니다.』

조국이에요, 하나님의 조국. 하나의 세계입니다. 세계의 나라가 둘이 아니에요. 하나입니다, 하나. 절대 하나입니다.

『오늘날 이 땅 위에 살고 있는 인간들은 하나님이 예고하셨던 그 나라와 그 의를 찾지 못하고 있습니다. 그래서 그 나라와 그 의를 찾는 것이 오늘날 우리 인류의 소망이요, 또한 지금까지 수천년 역사노정을 살다 간 인간들에게도 소망이었다는 것을 여러분들은 알아야 될 것입니다.』

여러분이에요. 레버런 문은 다 알고 있어요. ‘레버런 문은 독재자 입장에서 자기는 빼놓고 얘기했다.’ 할는지 모르지만, 빼놓고 얘기한 것은 자신 있다는 얘기예요.

『그러면 이런 소망의 그 나라, 소망의 그 의가 어찌하여 우리의 최후의 목표로서 남아지게 되었습니까? 그것은 인간이 타락했기 때문입니다. 인간 조상의 타락으로 말미암아 그 나라와 그 의의 중심이 될 수 있는 하나님과 인간이 아무런 관계를 맺을 수 없는 처지에 놓이게 되었습니다.』쫓겨났지요? 부정할 수 없어요.

『즉 그 나라와 그 의의 중심인 아버지와…』

하나님이 아버지예요. 아버지를 몰랐어요. 지금 뭐 선생님의 가르침을 받아 가지고 전부 혁명적으로 말하지만 말이에요.

『하나님 아버지와 가정과, 그리고 그 나라에 대하여 자세히 모르는 인간으로 전락되었기 때문에, 하나님께서는 이런 무지한 백성과 인류를 깨우쳐 그 하나님 아버지와 가정과 국가가 어떤 것인가를 가르쳐 주기 위하여 지금까지 역사노정에서 수고해 오셨습니다. 그래서 그 나라와 그 의를 찾아 세우는 것이 아직까지도 우리의 소망이요, 목표로 남아지게 된 것입니다.

이 세계에는 현재 수많은 나라가 존재하고 있습니다. 그러나 그 많은 국가들 가운데 하나님으로부터 정말 사랑을 받는 나라는 하나도 없습니다.』

미국이 하나님의 사랑을 받아요? 한의 나라예요. 근심의 나라예요.

『그러므로 이러한 타락세계를 부인하고 새로운 하나님의 나라를 다시 창조하지 않으면 안 된다고 하는 것이 지금까지 6천년간 하나님이 섭리해 오신 목적입니다. 그래서 하나님은 역사를 통해 나라를 찾는 섭리를 해 오신 것입니다. 나라가 협조 안 하면 하나님의 인류 구원에 대한 뜻은 이루어지지 않기 때문입니다.』

나라가 있어야 섭리가 완성됩니다. 알겠어요?

The Completion of One Heart, One Body, One Thought, One Harmony, and True Love
(Introducing the pastors attending the blessing ceremony and reporting on the four major events in December, with a prayer report by Chairman Yang Chang-shik)

The era has come where the spiritual and physical worlds can live together
What you need to know is that Heung-jin, Hyo-jin, and then Yeong-jin, even Hye-jin, among the sons and daughters of the teacher, four have gone to the spiritual world and are living as a blessed family with the four great saints, the five great saints, and the wise men. December 15, 2002 (Sunday), East Garden.
* This speech was given during the Sunday service and morning Hoon Dok Hae, and the title was added by the editor.
236 The Completion of One Heart, One Body, One Thought, One Harmony, and True Love

We have come to an era where the spiritual and physical worlds can unite to educate what we could not teach our children to serve the True Parents on earth and become filial sons and daughters.

Not only your couple but also your good ancestors, and if there are saints or sages born in that region, those saints and sages will come down with your good ancestors, blessed ancestors, to protect your blessed families.

Therefore, the spiritual and physical worlds are not separate worlds. Although your mind and body have become separate and peculiar, and the mind's person and the body's person are fighting, now that we have entered an era where the body and mind are united, it is not a time when heaven and earth are separated but a time of unification, where a new nation, Cheon Il Guk, a nation where two people become one, where the subject and object become one, and God can dwell in the center. This is the principle of creation.

Since this is the fundamental principle of the way of heaven, your life must be united around that principle. The body and mind must become one. The eyes are also in pairs. Everything is in pairs. Therefore, what is emphasized this year is that God is also One Heart, One Body, One Thought, and One Harmony. Your mind and body must become one. If the mind and body do not become one, no matter how much you are a blessed family, you cannot enter the heavenly world.

Those who have not united their body and mind must go to the other world and undergo a training process to unite their body and mind, receiving special training. They must undergo special training like a 100-day workshop or a 40-day workshop. It is shameful to do such dual work. Those who receive such dual education in the spiritual world belong to the archangel level. Although they have received the blessing.

237

Originally, the archangel has no ideal counterpart. They are not meant to receive the blessing. However, because the ancestors of humanity fell by receiving the body of the archangel on earth, they received the bloodline of the archangel and went to the other world with an ideal counterpart, but until now, they have all been separated. Even if a man or woman or parents go to the other world, they all remain in the realm according to their spiritual state. They have all been separated. Now the era of unification has come, the era of unification. The body and mind are united.

There is no way for the body and mind to become one without true love.

What unites the body and mind? The will, God's will. One Heart, One Body, One Thought... The body and mind are united through true love. There is no way to become one without true love.

Even the five senses, like your eyes, cannot become one without true love. There is no power to unite the physical five senses and the spiritual five senses except for true love. What is true love? True love is living for the sake of others, investing and forgetting.

Therefore, the power of true love is greater in output than input. In today's material world, the output is smaller than the input, but in true love, the output is greater than the input. If you invest ten and stop there, it does not go beyond that world. Therefore, the power of true love grows by investing ten, investing again, and continuing.

If you inflate a tube with air tightly, and there is a person here, and you push it with a board, if you push it to make a round, the pushing force causes it to rotate, and the pushing force acts, and because the counterpart absolutely lives for the subject, the more it moves, the more it increases. You must know that this power is in true love.

Therefore, when you feel joy, when the body and mind are united with true love and become joyful, no matter how joyful something in the world is, it is incomparable. Because there is such power that can resonate with the whole universe, only true love can unify the five senses of the spirit and body. Do you understand what I mean?

Who is God? God is my Father. He is not far away. He is more fundamental than the parents of the world. When you say God the Father, He embraces the world, embraces the entire created world, and as the representative center, He must experience the realm of heart that can be one with the invisible Father as a substantial son, more than substantial parents, for true love to start.

Since it has become such an era, the spiritual world is not another country. It is like the inside and outside. In terms of the hand, the mind is like the inside, and the body is like the outside. The mind is like the palm of this hand, and the body is like the outside, united. Even if it moves, it moves together, like the body and mind becoming one centered on true love, and thoughts becoming one. What is thought? What is One Thought? The '念' in One Thought (一念) is 'now (今)' under 'heart (心)'. It is the heart now. The heart now is seeking love, One Thought! The life of a lifetime is completing the path of true love.

Even individually, when the body and mind become one, as a man or woman, they are finding the path of completing their life of true love. A man or woman who can do that becomes a couple and finally finds God together.

Since you came from your parents, you must become one with the parents who gave birth to you, with the body and mind united. Since you came from your parents, you must become one with your parents. Because you came from true love, you can only find it through true love.

Therefore, what makes parents able to be parents? Parents themselves cannot stand in the position of father and mother. Only when they give birth to children, at the moment when the baby cries 'Aang!' can they have the position and love of parents. It is not the couple themselves who decide the parents as the owners of love. It is the children who decide the parents.

A man becomes the owner of love through his wife, and a wife becomes the owner of love through loving her husband. You must know this. A husband himself cannot be the owner of love. True love cannot exist without a counterpart.

You cannot walk the path of true love alone.

Therefore, even God, who created heaven and earth, cannot achieve the ideal of love alone. No matter how famous a president or saint or sage there is in the world, they cannot walk the path of completing true love alone.

Therefore, no matter how well a person lives alone, they are lonely. Even if they look in all directions, there is no world where they can settle down and rest. There is no nest of love. They must live centered on a counterpart. What counterpart? Not a counterpart of money. You cannot live happily alone with a bundle of money. You cannot live happily alone with a bundle of knowledge. The same goes for a bundle of power. These are auxiliary conditions, not the main conditions for which humans were born.

The only thing that can guide and manage the whole is true love. Therefore, individuals were born from parents, and they must unite their body and mind to respect and absolutely live for and love the parents with whom the body and mind are united. This is where the parent-child relationship unfolds.

Therefore, if you are born as a man or woman, you cannot help but be filial to your parents. The word 'filial piety' is unnecessary. From the time they are born in their mother's womb, the born children cannot be the owners. No matter how much a man or woman does, the origin is the parents. It is because the parents exist that they were born.

The existence of oneself began from true love, and the origin of true love is not oneself, nor is the origin of true life oneself. The origin of true life and true love is the parents, and since they were born as the fruit of the united love of the parents, the parents must live for their children more than themselves. Without children, there is no hope.

Therefore, parents hope that their beloved children will be several million times better than themselves. If a patient is about to die after passing the third stage of cancer, would you say they are dying? You should say they are getting better. You need to know that clearly.

Now, from the beginning of 'The Reality of the Spirit World'! From now on, do you want to be someone who doesn't know the spirit world or someone who knows it? "I want to be someone who knows it." Raise your hand if you want to be someone who doesn't know it. I'll kick you out to the gate. You'll be treated poorly. Why? Because, you rascals, who can enter the school gate if you become failures after being taught so well? Who will treat you well? It's impossible. Now! (Reading of the message sent from the spirit world by Mr. Lee Sang-heon ≪The Reality of the Spirit World and Earthly Life≫)

I will definitely become a citizen of the Kingdom of Heaven.

『1. A Letter to True Parents
"Parents, may you find comfort in receiving this child's letter."』

You all need to report to the teacher as well. You report, don't you? "I report." Right? "Yes." You should report when today is better than yesterday, not report bad things. You should add to it every day. It's the same. Since you are responsible for the spirit world and have gone there, you should report. Now!

『……Since you are working hard on earth, we are trying to organize and evangelize this heavenly place, but fundamentally, it seems that it will be completed only when True Parents come.』That's right. I need to go and clean it up completely. Now!

『……Father, during this time, this child has wandered the spirit world without rest. I have tried to search every nook and cranny to understand it.』If you don't believe that, you're in trouble. Distrust becomes a problem. Now!

『……In conclusion, to summarize the differences between earthly people and spirit world people, earthly people live under the constraints of limited space and time. They live busily to solve the problems of food, clothing, and shelter, making life difficult and exhausting. However, spirit world people are infinitely free because there are no constraints or obstacles in the spirit world. They have no worries about food, clothing, and shelter, so they are infinitely bright and humble. This applies when the result of their physical life is concluded as a citizen of the Kingdom of Heaven.』

Citizens of the Kingdom of Heaven! Say it. "Citizens of the Kingdom of Heaven!" I will definitely become a citizen of the Kingdom of Heaven! Say it. "I will definitely become a citizen of the Kingdom of Heaven!" You must do it on earth. You need to know how blessed it is to meet the teacher and receive teachings. If you live carelessly, it becomes a big problem. The resentment is great. Now!

『……The face is round like the earthly appearance, and long people remain long, but when they come to the spirit world, the face changes according to the earthly life, so those who polish their hearts to come to the Kingdom of Heaven are wise.』

Raise your hand if you want to be beautiful. Raise your hand if you want to be handsome. You must become someone who lives for others. If you say you will live for others for a thousand or ten thousand years, you will stay close to God, those who live for others. That is the mainstream ideology. Now!

『……I hope that the life of earthly people will be one that joyfully welcomes the season of fruition by bearing complete fruit between spirit and body.』

Stay still. Young-jun and Jin-man, make 250 lots for drawing. Write 60 numbers on them.

『……Chapter 3 Life in the Spirit World Viewed from the Principle』

Let's do that later. I told you to make the lots for drawing, bring them quickly. Tell Mother to bring the 60 things I mentioned in the morning.

Raise your hand if you haven't received the blessing here. Are you second generation? Are you second generation? "No." Haven't received the blessing? How old are you? "I'm twenty-two."

The people here haven't prepared breakfast, right? "We are making it now." How many? "250." "How should we mark the 60? Should we write numbers?" You should write numbers. "I'll write from number 1 to 60." Of course!

Sato, are you here? "Yes." How much fish is stored in the frozen company? Is there a lot? *How much frozen fish is there? "We brought it from Alaska." Don't you sell it here? (Laughter) "This is not for sale, it's for East Garden…." There isn't much of this, right? "There isn't anything good." There is a lot where you are, right? "Not that much. Just a little." How many is a little? "Two or three." Can two or three feed about 300 people? "Not that much." Then you need to buy it. I want to make sashimi here for breakfast one day. (*Spoken in Japanese)

Hyoyul, do you understand? One day sashimi, the next day potatoes, the next day sweet potatoes. Roots, then fruits. Eat fruits in the morning and give them one to take with them, doing it all like that. "You mean fruits?" There are many fruits, right? In America, valuable fruits can be bought in the East, right? Different fruits each time. If you eat fruits, how many trees are there where you plant the seeds in your hometown? You need to plant the seeds. Hyoyul, do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

A commemorative item for the new transition era centered on Cheon Il Guk

For 14 days until the morning of the 29th. Until the morning of the 29th, then the teacher must leave for Korea. In Korea, there is a big task to do. Those who are over 40 years old and have graduated from university in Korea, Japan, and the United States for more than six months are supposed to attend. That is a special privilege. Then they study. After studying for 60 to 70 days…. Parents' birthday is February 6, right? How many days from today? "From today, it's exactly 50 days left." If it's 50 days, until February 16, until February, I don't know what will be done in Korea. For the liberation of the homeland.

These are the ties the teacher has had until now. As a commemorative gift, those who receive this must make a name card centered on their name. The name will appear in the middle of the name card, right? I'll distribute these one by one, and at that time, bring your name card and get the teacher's signature. I plan to sign on the back of that name card. That's the commemoration. Take a photo with the tie and the signed name card and keep it as a record. Understand?

"What kind of name card?" Your name! "Do you mean the Cheon Il Guk certificate?" No, your name! If it's Kim Hyoyul, it's Cheon Il Guk Kim Hyoyul. "Do the people who are drawn make the card?" If the people who are drawn bring a name card, since they have their name, the teacher will sign it, and you should take a photo with the signed name card and tie and keep it. For 14 days, a commemorative item for the new transition era centered on Cheon Il Guk is given. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

This one will be something you can't buy with money when it becomes a hundred or a thousand years. A hundred years will pass without a problem, right? Will it or won't it? "It will." It depends on how you keep it. There are numbers on all of them. The number will come out, right? After that, things like Mother's clothes or items Mother had, things Parents had, will be distributed as gifts. To those who have diligently attended the Hoon Dok Hae.

From now on, you must become someone who loves the spirit world more than anyone else. Those who don't know the spirit world will be eliminated. We all need to know this. You must read it every day and know it clearly, so when you see the spirit world, you can say, 'This is related in such a way, so when I go to that world, I will influence it in such and such a way, correct what needs to be corrected, and guide what needs to be guided.'

When you go, you will become the elder sister and brother of the blessed families of the saints and sages of the spirit world. It's your older sister's family. You must be a model for them. Those people don't have these commemorative items, right? The items True Parents used are being passed down. Of course, the words are the words, but how glorious it is to have the living items used in the world? To boast about it in the spirit world, how diligently must you attend the Hoon Dok Hae, and how diligently must you live your faith life?

You can't register in Cheon Il Guk without being a blessed family.

Now, draw lots. Don't do it one by one, share it among many people and do it quickly. Don't do it alone, share and do it. (Drawing lots)

Those who haven't received the blessing should stop. Pass it on. If you're not a blessed family, pass it on. The blessed family is precious. You don't know how precious the blessing is, do you? It's a bloodline conversion. Without being a blessed family, you can't register in Cheon Il Guk. Cheon Il Guk! Say it. "Cheon Il Guk!" Cheon Il Guk (天一國) is a nation (國) where two (二) people (人) become one (一), and then it becomes Won Il Guk (圓一國) centered on three generations. It's a 'round won (圓)' one nation. Then a unified world, a unified nation comes out. Cheon Il Guk, Won Il Guk, Unified Nation, it must develop.

Without completing the three object purpose and the four position foundation, it can't become Won Il Guk. It's where up and down, front and back, left and right become completely one.

Is it done? "Yes." Is there any left? It doesn't seem to be 250 people. I counted them all. "There are a few left." What's ten? It's more than 20. "There are eighteen left." Quickly call the people at East Garden. The people here listen to the Hoon Dok Hae every day while working. "Come quickly." If they don't come quickly, they'll be excluded. (Laughter) Between couples, one pair should take one each. You can't take two. Didn't you take two each here? Quickly, quickly take them.

Now, open them. Number 1, number 2… line up in order. Tell Mother to come down. "There were many left in this box."

See how many numbers are there. "Nine." Nine, raise your hand if you were born in January. Both lunar and solar are fine. Come out. If you're not a blessed family, don't come out. Why are there so many? Play rock-paper-scissors. (One family comes out after playing rock-paper-scissors) Take one from here. Take any one. What number is it? "Number 1." (Applause) (People born from February to December gather and play rock-paper-scissors to draw lots)

Now, line up in order from number 1. Now, Mother should give them. These are good ties. (Distributing ties) Is it all done? You need to make name cards. When you make them and bring them, the teacher will sign them, and you should take a photo with the tie and keep it. Understand? "Yes."

You need to make your business card. When you make it and bring it, you should take a photo with the commemorative item and the signed name card and keep it. Name cards are necessary, right? (Explanation about name cards by Chairman Kim Hyoyul) Write Cheon Il Guk year 2 on it and your name. (Bows) (Three cheers) *
